[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Summary[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mA stack-buffer-overflow vulnerability has been detected in the Wireshark ICMP [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdissector during fuzzing with AddressSanitizer. The issue occurs in the [0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`dissect_interface_identification_object` function when processing ICMP extension [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mheaders, specifically involving a [0m[1;36m256[0m[39m-byte write operation that overflows a [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m128[0m[39m-byte stack buffer named `ident_name.i`.[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Description[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Vulnerability Type[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThis is a **stack-buffer-overflow** vulnerability with a SCARINESS score of [0m[1;36m60[0m[39m, [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mclassified as a multi-byte-write-stack-buffer-overflow. The vulnerability allows [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwriting beyond the bounds of a stack-allocated buffer.[0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### What the Issue Is[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe AddressSanitizer detected a write operation of [0m[1;36m256[0m[39m bytes at address [0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;36m0x7fef55473aa0[0m[39m`, which exceeds the bounds of the allocated stack buffer. The stack[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mframe analysis reveals:[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- A buffer `ident_name.i` allocated at offset [0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m32[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m160[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, providing only [0m[1;36m128[0m[39m bytes [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mof space [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m902[0m[39m in packet-icmp.c[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- A write operation attempting to copy [0m[1;36m256[0m[39m bytes via `memcpy`[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The memory access at offset [0m[1;36m160[0m[39m overflows into adjacent stack variables including[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`afi.i`, `addr_length.i`, `tf_entry.i`, and `tf_object`[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Call Stack Analysis[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe vulnerability is triggered through the following execution path:[0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Entry Point**: The fuzzer calls `LLVMFuzzerTestOneInput` in fuzzshark.c[0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Dissection Chain**: [0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - `epan_dissect_run` → `dissect_record` → `dissect_frame`[0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - `call_dissector_work` routes to the ICMP dissector[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - `dissect_icmp` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mpacket-icmp.c[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m is invoked[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Vulnerable Function**: [0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - `dissect_icmp_extension` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mpacket-icmp.[0m[1;92mc:971[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m creates the stack frame with the [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mundersized buffer[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - `dissect_interface_identification_object` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mpacket-icmp.[0m[1;92mc:927[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m calls [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`tvb_memcpy`[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - `tvb_memcpy` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mtvbuff.[0m[1;92mc:945[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m performs the actual memcpy operation[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Overflow**: `__asan_memcpy` detects the [0m[1;36m256[0m[39m-byte write exceeding the [0m[1;36m128[0m[39m-byte [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbuffer[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Important Observations[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Buffer Size Mismatch**: The stack buffer `ident_name.i` is allocated with [0m[1;36m128[0m[39m [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbytes but the code attempts to copy [0m[1;36m256[0m[39m bytes into it[0m                               [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Adjacent variables being partially underflowed/overflowed[0m                      [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_snippets[0m[39m>[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Analysis of the Vulnerability[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mAfter examining the code snippets and evaluation report, I've identified the root [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcause of the stack-buffer-overflow:[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Core Issue[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe `dissect_interface_identification_object` function at line [0m[1;36m927[0m[39m in [0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`epan/dissectors/packet-icmp.c` performs an unbounded copy:[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```c[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mtvb_memcpy[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtvb, ident_name, offset, obj_length - [0m[1;36m4[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mWhere:[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- `ident_name` is a [0m[1;36m128[0m[39m-byte stack buffer [0m[1;39m([0m[39mdefined by `ICMP_MAX_IDENT_NAME_LENGTH`[0m[1;39m)[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- `obj_length` is read directly from the packet as a uint16_t [0m[1;39m([0m[39mcan be up to [0m[1;36m65535[0m[1;39m)[0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- No validation ensures `obj_length - [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m` doesn't exceed [0m[1;36m128[0m[39m bytes[0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Critical Observations[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Unnecessary memcpy**: The memcpy serves no actual purpose. Line [0m[1;36m933[0m[39m uses [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`proto_tree_add_item` which reads directly from the tvbuff safely. The intermediate[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcopy is redundant.[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Broken validation loop**: Lines [0m[1;36m929[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m931[0m[39m attempt to validate printability but [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mjust break on the first non-printable character without taking any action, making [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mit completely useless.[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Inconsistent with codebase patterns**: Every other object dissector in the [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfile [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`dissect_mpls_extended_payload_object`, `dissect_mpls_stack_entry_object`, [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`dissect_interface_information_object`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m follows a safe pattern using [0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`obj_trunc_length = [0m[1;35mMIN[0m[1;39m([0m[39mobj_length, [0m[1;35mtvb_reported_length_remaining[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtvb, offset[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`.[0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Similar code exists elsewhere**: Lines [0m[1;36m868[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m882[0m[39m in [0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`dissect_interface_information_object` show the correct way to handle [0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mvariable-length name strings without memcpy - using `proto_tree_add_item` directly [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwith proper bounds checking.[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Primary Approach: Remove Unnecessary memcpy [0m[1;39m([0m[39mRecommended[0m[1;39m)[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Location**: `epan/dissectors/packet-icmp.c` lines [0m[1;36m925[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m934[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Changes**:[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Remove the `ident_name` buffer declaration [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m902[0m[1;39m)[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Remove the `tvb_memcpy` call [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m927[0m[1;39m)[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Remove the broken printability validation loop [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m929[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m931[0m[1;39m)[0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Keep only the `proto_tree_add_item` call with proper bounds validation [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m933[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Implementation Steps**:[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Add `obj_trunc_length` calculation after reading `obj_length`:[0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   ```c[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   obj_length = [0m[1;35mtvb_get_ntohs[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtvb, offset[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   obj_trunc_length = [0m[1;35mMIN[0m[1;39m([0m[39mobj_length, [0m[1;35mtvb_reported_length_remaining[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtvb, offset[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   ```[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Replace the ICMP_EXT_ECHO_IDENT_NAME case [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m925[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m934[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m with:[0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   ```c[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   case ICMP_EXT_ECHO_IDENT_NAME:[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mobj_trunc_length > [0m[1;36m4[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m           [0m[1;35mproto_tree_add_item[0m[1;39m([0m[39mext_object_tree, hf_icmp_int_ident_name_string, [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                             tvb, offset, obj_trunc_length - [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m, ENC_ASCII[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       break;[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   ```[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Remove the `ident_name` buffer declaration from line [0m[1;36m902[0m[39m since it's no longer [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mneeded.[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Justification**:[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- This approach completely eliminates the vulnerability by removing the unsafe [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmemcpy[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- It follows the established pattern used throughout the codebase[0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- `proto_tree_add_item` with `ENC_ASCII` safely handles string display without [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mrequiring a stack buffer[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The printability validation is unnecessary - Wireshark's display engine handles [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mnon-printable characters appropriately[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Simpler code is less prone to bugs[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Alternative Approach: Add Bounds Checking [0m[1;39m([0m[39mIf memcpy must be retained[0m[1;39m)[0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mIf there's an undocumented requirement to validate the data before display, add [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mproper bounds checking:[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Changes**:[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Add `obj_trunc_length` calculation[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Limit copy size to minimum of `obj_trunc_length - [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m` and [0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`ICMP_MAX_IDENT_NAME_LENGTH`[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Fix the validation loop to use the actual copied length[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Implementation**:[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```c[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcase ICMP_EXT_ECHO_IDENT_NAME:[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    obj_trunc_length = [0m[1;35mMIN[0m[1;39m([0m[39mobj_length, [0m[1;35mtvb_reported_length_remaining[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtvb, offset[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mobj_trunc_length > [0m[1;36m4[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        uint32_t copy_length = [0m[1;35mMIN[0m[1;39m([0m[39mobj_trunc_length - [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m, [0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mICMP_MAX_IDENT_NAME_LENGTH[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m[1;35mtvb_memcpy[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtvb, ident_name, offset, copy_length[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m[35m/[0m[39m* Validate printability *[0m[35m/[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        bool all_printable = true;[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        for [0m[1;39m([0m[39munsigned i = [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m; i < copy_length; i++[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            if [0m[1;39m([0m[39m![0m[1;35mg_ascii_isprint[0m[1;39m([0m[39mident_name[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mi[0m[1;39m][0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                all_printable = false;[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                break;[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m[1;35mproto_tree_add_item[0m[1;39m([0m[39mext_object_tree, hf_icmp_int_ident_name_string, [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                          tvb, offset, obj_trunc_length - [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m, ENC_ASCII[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    break;[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mHowever, **this approach is NOT recommended** because the validation serves no [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpurpose and adds complexity.[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Preservation of Existing Logic[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe fix preserves all critical functionality:[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- ICMP extension parsing continues to work correctly[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Interface identification objects are still dissected and displayed[0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The display output remains the same [0m[1;39m([0m[39mproto_tree_add_item handles the display[0m[1;39m)[0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- All other code paths [0m[1;39m([0m[39mINDEX and ADDRESS c_types[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m remain unchanged[0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The fuzzing harness continues to work as-is[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Addressing Side Effects[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Potential concerns**:[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Loss of validation**: The printability check is removed, but [0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`proto_tree_add_item` with `ENC_ASCII` already handles non-printable characters [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mappropriately in Wireshark's UI.[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Behavior change**: The displayed data might include the full length from [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtvbuff rather than being truncated at [0m[1;36m128[0m[39m bytes. This is actually correct behavior [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- there's no reason to artificially limit the display to [0m[1;36m128[0m[39m bytes when more data [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mis available.[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **RFC compliance**: RFC [0m[1;36m8335[0m[39m doesn't specify a maximum length for the [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39midentification name field. The [0m[1;36m128[0m[39m-byte limit appears to be an arbitrary [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mimplementation choice, not a protocol requirement.[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Similar Patterns in Codebase[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe recommended fix follows patterns already established in the same file:[0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- `dissect_mpls_extended_payload_object` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m638[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m656[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m: Uses `obj_trunc_length` [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwith `proto_tree_add_item`[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- `dissect_interface_information_object` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m868[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m882[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m: Handles name strings [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwithout memcpy[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- `dissect_mpls_stack_entry_object` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m684[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m751[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m: Uses `obj_trunc_length` and [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`obj_end_offset` for bounds checking[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThese functions demonstrate that the safe pattern is well-established and trusted [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39min the Wireshark codebase.[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m
